Be prepared to be punished if you don't put a name tag on- yep 30 burpees and this is even if you are not able to physically do one burpee on your second day in the program and you will not be told that you are required to put a name tag on every single day. You may or may not be told you can modify a push up, a plank or a burpee but be prepared that you may get reprimanded and penalized if you do modify an exercise.  No time to work up to  being able to perform a required routine, do it and do it strong or be called out and humiliated.  Are coaches told to hone in on certain people to get them to drop out.  I am thinking yes- after all then the owners get to keep the clients $400.00 without that client even taking up a position in the class.  I wondered how this gym makes money if they give back the money paid up front - at least $400.00 if you lose 20 pounds..well after spending two days- minus five minutes when I walked out- I am pretty sure I know.  I wish everyone injured or put into a medical emergency in this program would post here- and don't ever think about getting your money back or having anyone who works at this gym or is a business partner in this gym understanding any of its downfalls.  After all - they are getting rich!< /text>

Simply the best Peruvian food you could possibly try. My family and friends try to come here every weekend because the delicious food keeps bringing us back. The service was good even when it got busy with people who also go there for the amazing food. < Review>
My family and I have been staying here since we relocated to the Sacramento area in June, and I have to say it has been an amazing experience. We didn't really know what to expect seeing as how "trailer parks" are notorious for being crazy but that's not the case at this location. From day one the manager Mario has been super helpful, even meeting us outside of business hours when we were available to come down and see the park before we officially moved. They have been more than accommodating on several occasions since our arrival as well. It is quiet and calm, my kids love the nice clean pool, and we are more comfortable here than I ever thought we would be. I havn't had to worry about my children's safety, or anybody touching or taking our things either (which are standard worries for any densely populated area). All in all, I am very glad we chose this park to be at while we were making this huge transition to a new area and appreciate how well maintained everything here is!< /Review>

< review>
As a parent of a team gymnast, I can not say enough good things about Airborne after experiencing 2 other competing gyms in the area. Airborne and its team coaches are dedicated to the girls and their success. The feedback my daughter receives while being coached is always done in a positive manner. The facility is regularly sanitized and exceptionally clean with health and safety being top priority at the gym. Airborne is our daughter‚Äôs ‚Äúhappy place‚Äù. She loves gymnastics and Airborne is the perfect fit for her and our family.</review>

< text>
My son has attended Airborne's Mini Mach, Mach 1 and now their Mach 2 parkour classes. He also has celebrated 2 birthdays there. Those alone are worth 4 stars.

However, the reason why I gave 5 stars and why I recommend them to anyone who has a kid who needs to get some energy out: when the restrictions were lifted and we came back for class and camps, they were so excited to see my son. < text>
I came here for a birthday party.

Parking is difficult!  It is in an office complex and I wasn't sure if I was parking in an approved spot or not.

The party was for 5 to 6 yr olds.  There was a separate sign in table for the birthday.  It would be helpful to know in advance that the children need to be barefoot, as some of the girls came wearing tights.  The staff was attentive to the kids.  There were bleachers on 1 side of the gym, where the parents could sit and watch.

After the play, the party continued upstairs.  There was additional bleacher  seating in front of a large window where you could see the entire gym floor below. There were also additional bathrooms upstairs.

The kids had a great time and the parents had an opportunity to talk.<//text>

<review>This review is relative to other McDonald's locations.
Food quality is standard for the chain.
Accuracy is good, so they get your order correct almost every time.  However, if you want ketchup for your fries, etc, you better ask.
It seems as though many of the workers are not highly fluent in English and really don't seem to care much about the customers.  They do not go out of their way to make you feel appreciated but are not overtly rude.
The property is usually not clean.
The lobby is small and often occupied with people who appear to have just left a shelter.  The lot is also small and usually full, so don't expect to park.
If you choose the drive through, which is the preferred way, be wary of the fact that you will likely need to approach and line up on Jackson street from 13th as there is only enough room for 1 car before the order speaker.
Expect to be approached by one of the panhandlers who take rotating shifts and are ignored by the staff.<//review>< Pics>

< Text>
Food is OK. McDonald's menu almost never changes. I like their Gilroy garlic fries - only if you don't mind them soggy after they are soaked in garlic and cheese.
There are two issues with this place:
1. There are only eight or so parking spots in the lot. Once full you'll be feeding the meters on the streets. Since this is near downtown it'll be almost impossible to find a spot. And if you find a spot you'll be adding $3-6 to your cheap McDonald's meal.
2. Lot's and lots of transient people hanging around the area. It can be dangerous. One time I was taking a picture of the nearby post office. A guy threatened to beat me up because he thought I was taking his picture.</Text>
